(_( a_DT )_) Bovine_NNP vaccine_NN lymph_NN can_MD be_VB used_VBN fresh_JJ only_RB where_WRB there_EX is_VBZ an_DT establishment_NN in_IN which_WDT the_DT calves_NNS can_MD be_VB inoculated_VBN and_CC children_NNS vaccinated_VBN on_IN the_DT premises_NNS direct_VBP from_IN the_DT calf_NN ._.

(_( b_NN )_) The_DT preservation_NN of_IN the_DT lymph_NN is_VBZ therefore_RB necessary_JJ :_: this_DT can_MD be_VB done_VBN in_IN two_CD ways_NNS ,_, namely_RB ,_, by_IN admixture_NN with_IN lanoline_NN or_CC by_IN solution_NN in_IN a_DT mixture_NN of_IN glycerine_NN and_CC water_NN ._.
There_EX may_MD possibly_RB be_VB other_JJ means_NNS of_IN preserving_VBG it_PRP ,_, but_CC we_PRP are_VBP only_RB concerned_JJ with_IN these_DT two_CD methods_NNS ._.
(_( c_NN )_) The_DT first_JJ is_VBZ easy_JJ ,_, rapid_JJ and_CC cheap_JJ ,_, but_CC it_PRP is_VBZ open_JJ to_TO various_JJ objections_NNS ;_: and_CC is_VBZ used_VBN in_IN the_DT Shillong_NNP dep√¥t_NN ,_, only_RB for_IN the_DT preparation_NN of_IN virus_NN intended_VBN to_TO be_VB used_VBN in_IN the_DT dep√¥t_NN itself_PRP for_IN inoculating_VBG calves_NNS :_: the_DT small_JJ pots_NNS in_IN which_WDT the_DT mixture_NN is_VBZ kept_VBN are_VBP emptied_VBN at_IN one_CD time_NN ,_, each_DT calf_NN having_VBG a_DT separate_JJ pot_NN ,_, and_CC these_DT pots_NNS are_VBP not_RB allowed_VBN to_TO be_VB opened_VBN ,_, part_NN of_IN the_DT contents_NNS used_VBN and_CC the_DT rest_NN kept_VBD for_IN a_DT future_JJ occasion_NN ._.

(_( d_NN )_) If_IN lanoline_JJ lymph_NN were_VBD supplied_VBN to_TO district_NN vaccinators_NNS ,_, they_PRP would_MD have_VB to_TO carry_VB their_PRP$ opened_VBN pots_NNS about_IN with_IN them_PRP ,_, setting_VBG them_PRP down_RP on_IN the_DT ground_NN ,_, in_IN the_DT sunshine_NN ,_, in_IN the_DT dust_NN ,_, any-_NN where_WRB ,_, putting_VBG in_IN a_DT dirty_NN or_CC bloody_NN lancet_NN from_IN time_NN to_TO time_NN ,_, and_CC ,_, in_IN fact_NN ,_, exposing_VBG the_DT virus_NN to_TO various_JJ chances_NNS of_IN deterioration_NN ._.
(_( e_NN )_) For_IN district_NN use_NN therefore_IN the_DT second_JJ form_NN of_IN preservation_NN is_VBZ solely_RB used_VBN ._.
The_DT vaccine_NN matter_NN as_IN scraped_VBN from_IN the_DT abdomens_NNS of_IN the_DT vaccinifers_NNS is_VBZ pounded_VBN up_RP with_IN a_DT mixture_NN of_IN glycerine_NN and_CC water_NN in_IN the_DT proportion_NN of_IN 2_CD parts_NNS of_IN the_DT solid_JJ matter_NN ,_, and_CC 1_CD part_NN each_DT of_IN glycerine_NN and_CC water_NN ,_, by_IN weight_NN ._.

(_( f_NN )_) The_DT advantages_NNS of_IN this_DT plan_NN are_VBP many_JJ and_CC obvious_JJ :_: there_EX is_VBZ no_DT possibility_NN of_IN foreign_JJ matter_NN getting_VBG mixed_JJ with_IN the_DT virus_NN ,_, it_PRP can_MD not_RB be_VB contaminated_VBN by_IN a_DT part_NN being_VBG laid_VBN on_IN the_DT arm_NN of_IN a_DT child_NN and_CC a_DT portion_NN of_IN this_DT then_RB put_VB back_RB into_IN the_DT mass_NN ;_: each_DT child_NN receives_VBZ the_DT contents_NNS of_IN one_CD tube_NN :_: the_DT virus_NN is_VBZ kept_VBN hermetically_RB sealed_VBN and_CC the_DT atmosphere_NN can_MD have_VB no_DT effect_NN on_IN it_PRP ._.

I_PRP presume_VBP the_DT reason_NN to_TO be_VB that_IN the_DT glycerine_NN ,_, which_WDT at_IN first_RB rapidly_RB destroys_VBZ all_DT extraneous_JJ germs_NNS ,_, in_IN time_NN renders_NNS the_DT vaccine_NN virus_NN itself_PRP sterile_JJ and_CC inert_NN ._.
